< Review>
The food here is amazing! I've tried the beef stew and highly recommend it..the beef really melts in your mouth and falls apart...its heavenly. The grilled salmon with fried rice in garlic butter sauce is wonderful...salmon is good, and the rice is amazing. My husband tried the filet mignon is very tender and comes with a really savory butter herb topping and nice sides. All in all the portions are very generous and the food well presented and DELICIOUS.  Everyone in our group was very impressed and very full upon leaving! The staff is polite and the ambiance is beautiful and clean. This place is new and the owners take feedback to improve very well. I think that the restaurant has been pretty popular and seen some rush hours where they were a bit understaffed which is why some other reviewers were dissatisfied...but I'm guessing first month growing pains that management will address. Even more than the restaurant itself...the staff and management is very solid and attentative and I imagine it will only get better from here. Highly recommend!

On another note, the sandwich takeaway area just opened this week and the bread they bake is one of the best I've had. I got to talk to some of the staff and they mentioned that they try to use as many natural products and forgo harmful chemicals in their bread making process. The bread has a slightly different texture than other bakeries in the area, but tastes WAAAY better in my opinion. It more authentic French baguette style than the spongier Vietnamese style bread.

I also found that if the sandwich takeaway area is closed, you can still go into the restaurant side to order things that are already made, from the sandwich side.

Edit: We came back again and ordered the beef stew (again) and the halibut...omg if you like butter this is halibut is to die for...I gotta know how they make it taste like that! My husband ordered it and I ate more than half his plate haha. The beef stew was delicious and slightly different than the first time I ordered it...it was definitely better this time around. It's great to know they're constantly improving their dishes.< /Review>

<Review>I've posted a review several times in the past (February and March!) and it keeps disappearing! But I love this place enough to come back and try again.

After a really rough breakup, my friends encouraged me to head in and trade in some old jewelry from my past relationship. Al, Mary, and Angela were there to encourage me, reminding me about Jeremiah 29:11--that God had a plan for me. They also helped me find a tangible reminder--a watermelon tourmaline ring that signified the hope I had for a great future. It was a symbolic moment, trading in the old for the new.

Later, when this great future was being realized, my future husband and I went into Jewelry to Go to check out engagement rings and wedding sets. With many diverse options to choose from, an engagement ring and wedding band stuck out right from the beginning. It was gorgeous! There was only one thing--I didn't absolutely love the round center stone.

Unbeknownst to me, my future fiance went back into Jewelry to Go to discuss changing the diamond. After much research, he told them he wanted an asscher cut diamond. Because they didn't have the perfect diamond in their store, they offered to look for the right diamond while they were out of the country for a jewelry show. My diamond was handpicked and brought back from another country just to fit in my beautiful ring. Not only did they go out of their way to find the perfect diamond, they also were able to quickly change the diamonds in the ring. They also worked with my husband to figure out finances.

My husband proposed the night he picked it up because he was so excited for me to see the beautiful ring Jewelry to Go had created. Guess what!? I said yes!

My ring is stunning and I get compliments everywhere we go! I also have Pandora beads for each of the big events that have happened since. Jewelry to Go has found a place in our family as our family jeweler. We are so thankful for a jewelry store that can be a part of each momentous occasion that comes in our future.

Thanks, Al, Mary, Angela, and staff!!</Review><pictures>None<//pictures>< response>

< Text>
I took my rather expensive Tissot Swiss watch in to Jewelry to Go to have the sapphire crystal replaced.  The jeweler quoted me over $200 to replace the crystal, which is a job the Tissot factory charges $45 for (it takes up to 7 weeks to get your watch back though) so rather than spend 7 weeks without my watch, I opted to use Jewelry to Go.

When I got my watch back, it was missing one of the retaining bands.  The jeweler said that he had lost it during the repair, but assured me that he would find it and call me (this was nearly 3 months ago and he hasn't called).

While I was waiting for him to find the band, I looked through the store at some of the loose diamonds.  The jeweler came back out and showed me a couple of very overpriced diamonds (example: 1 carat diamond of average color and clarity he wanted $10,000 for) and one of them he took out of the plastic sleeve and handed to me.  I looked at the diamond and then turned the packaging over to see the specifics and the price.  Because he had removed the plastic sleeve, the diamond fell off the packaging and onto to the counter with a soft "tink" sound to which prompted  the jeweler to literally scream "BE CAREFUL" in my face.  After that I wiped his spit from my forehead and left his shop; I haven't been back since.< /Text>

<Rating>5</Rating>< Text>
My now husband bought me the engagement ring of my dreams. It is a Tacori set and he had to go out of town to buy it. The ring was a bit too big and not wearing it wasnt an option for me, I set out to find a temporary fix.

I went to a local jeweler and they said they could clamp a metal temporary sizer on the ring. I agreed and they clamped the sizer on. The second it was back in my hand I thought it had been ruined forever! There were deep scratches and dents all over the platnium ring! My eyes filled with tears instantly! I was told this was a normal thing to happen and I should have known. I left with a broken heart.

As I was driving home, I saw Jewelry To Go through my tears and wondered why I hadn't gone there in the first place. I walked in and Angie was the first to greet me and comfort me. She told me that her dad, Al could look at it and let me know what could be done. Within a few minutes my ring was being examined by Al. He assured me that he could make it better and he did. Within fifteen minutes I had my ring back in my hands in almost new condition. I want to add, I was not charged a dime!

The entire Alvarado family mended my broken heart that day, and they did it out of the kindness of their hearts. They restored my faith in jewelrs in this community. I don't think I could ever thank them enough!

On our wedding day my husband surprised me with a beautiful diamond necklace and earrings from none other than Jewelry To Go!<//Text>

<date>1603397937279</date><Rate>1</Rate><review>Buyer beware!   I was extremely disappointed in the deceptive advertising used  by this dealer.   The advertised price for the Jeep I was interested in was reasonable and led me to reach out to them.  When I called to express my interest, I was told that the real price of the Jeep was approximately $7,000 higher than advertised!  According to the dealer, the lower advertised price did not include accessories that were already installed on the vehicle, and the additional $7,000 was to pay for these accessories.  From my perspective, an open and honest dealer would have identified these accessories and the higher price--which were already known--up front in the advertisement.   This was a classic "bait and switch"  deceptive marketing trick--use a low price to get my interest and then drop the higher price on me once I was lured in. Unfortunately, we don't control what third-party transportation companies charge, a list factors go into the cost, first it is your location, current gas prices, etc. Lastly, there's a few items that go into a contract that are inevitable, city taxes according to your location, governments fees. I do understand your disappointment but please know sometimes our hands are tied as a dealership since these fees are out of our control. I hope this helps explain how things work and what our intentions are. We are here to serve and would love another opportunity in the future, if you desire. < Text>
I took my cat in as she was having bladder issues.  My regular vet treated her a couple of weeks ago but she relapsed and couldn't pee.  Since they were closing when I called they said to take her to emergency.  Called Sage and they said to bring her in and call when I got there.  After I got there, about 5:10pm on Saturday, and checked her in over the phone, it took an hour for them to see her.  They never told me there the wait would be that long so we just sat in the car.  When the doctor finally examined her and called me, she rattled off a list of things she recommended, (medicine, x-rays, blood/urine tests) to the tune of over $1000.  I said to just give her enough medicine for a day and I would take her back to her regular vet.  When I went to check her out it was well over $300, $168 being the office visit,  $110 for one medicine plus a 2nd medicine, which I can't remember the price of.  I was shocked and expressed it.  The doctor gave me a discount to just under $300.  I verified that I was only getting enough medicine for Sunday as I already had an appointment for Monday morning with her vet and they said it was only enough to get me through a couple of days.  I paid the bill and went home.  The time spent there was 2 hours, with 30 minutes just waiting to get my cat back.  The bill was supposed to be emailed but still haven't received it and it's the next morning.  Never going back.</Text>

<Text>I am writing this review after losing my dog, cremating him, and having spent $977.64 here on two visits.
I do not recommend this place, and am now averse even to traveling to Dublin because of my depressing experience here.

The care received for the $977.64 included two consultations, a subcutaneous injection of fluid (which pet owners can do themselves), and an IV drip that lasted less than an hour. My dog never got life-saving care, though my family and I waited outside this office for two entire afternoons.

During our second visit, our dog waited for 1.5 hours outside before he was seen. After calling their supervisor to try to ask what was going on and tell them that another vet had said my dog needed fluids ASAP, the supervisor spoke to me unpleasantly and condescendingly, explaining how my dog needing fluid therapy was of less concern than a dog with heart failure.  I understand this, but when my dog was later seen, we were told he was dying.

Hence, while I waited in a car with my dog and called repeatedly to advocate for his care, my dog was dying at the doorstep of this ER. This is different from another ER I went to (Beacon Vet in Fremont, where my dog eventually passed), as they had a COVID protocol where a vet tech would wait outside to triage a pet. SAGE seemed to rely on some amount of self-triage / triage done through the phone, and that disappointed me.

When we were finally seen, they did not proceed with the care we had hoped for and told us to euthanize (with some pressure), because his kidneys were failing. While I can understand SAGE may have thought his case was futile,   other vets at Banfield on that day and the *next* day thought that my dog still had a chance. He just needed fluid therapy, which he had previously responded well.

I am unhappy with SAGE because my dog didn't get much care or attention here for the $977.64 that evaporated while we tried to save him. I regret driving cities over for SAGE and wish I had gone to the local ER.

I also wish I had my dog back, but nothing's going to change that.</Text>< pictures>

< Review>
I wish I could give Sage a lower rating! I called them as I was rushing my new malamute puppy over (since my vet was already closed for the night). My puppy ingested a small condiment container (that I thought was out of her reach) and I knew I had to get her to emergency ASAP.  We had a rough 15 minute window to get to the emergency so they could induce vomiting to get the condiment container out otherwise it would be further along her digestive tract and would lead to complications and maybe surgery. When I called and spoke to the staff at Sage - they said they didn't have a wait and even if they did when I arrived, they would ensure she was taken back immediately to get the process started. When I arrived, I wasn't acknowledged.  I tried to get the attention of the staff but couldn't as they were socializing amongst themselves. The waiting room was empty except for another couple waiting for their dog to be discharged. As soon as I approached the counter, I was impolitely told to "hold on". I stood there and waited for about 5-7 minutes and at this point the 15 minute window to induce vomiting was almost up - I started to get anxious! I apologized and interrupted the staff to asked how much longer will I have to wait and pressed the time that we had left to induce vomiting. The staff rolled her eyes at me and sighed while her co-worker smirked - I was shocked! She said she had to register me into their system and started asking me various questions. I kindly asked if I could send my puppy back while I complete the registration process and she said "no". The registration took roughly 3-5 minutes and then she told me to wait and they'll take my puppy back when they're free - no ETA or sense of urgency. The thought of waiting longer and allowing the possibility of further complications made me extremely nervous. I decided to quickly search on my phone for other emergency vet's in the area and I found IronHorse Vet Care (down the street). I called them (while I was in the waiting area Sage) and asked if they have a current wait time and they said they do but also that doesn't matter typically because each pet is assessed differently based on whats going on. After I told them what happened - they told me to come immediately. I got up and started to walk out and the staff saw me but didn't ask if I was going to step outside or if I will be returning? I felt so uncomfortable but I pushed that feeling aside and quickly got my puppy into the car and drove to IronHorse!

When I arrived at IronHorse VetCare the staff, nurse, and doctor were waiting for me in the lobby as I pulled up. They took my puppy in the back right away! They could sense how stressed I was and offered me water/coffee/tea and to take a few minutes to sit/relax and breathe before they started the process to register her.  I didn't even finish the registration process - when the doctor came out to show me the condiment container (TMI - but they wanted to ensure it was exactly what she ate and reassure me that they got it out). I was literally in and out so fast and the service was so personal compared to SAGE!

I finally got a call back from Sage that night (about 45 minutes later) saying they're ready to take my puppy back and that she might need x-rays etc.. because of the time that had elapsed.

I couldn't believe (1) how long they waited to finally take her in when they told me that they would see her immediately upon my arrival. (2) The delay, rudeness, and lack of urgency from the front staff could've potentially caused severe complications for my puppy and cost me a lot of money (3) how bad my first experience was there and how I am never returning. I continue to tell all of my friends and family (and they've shared to their community) to save themselves of the stress and injustice  of going to Sage!

I highly recommend taking your pet to a more professional and genuine establishment (like IronHorse VetCare - NOT SAGE) that truly respects, cares, and empathizes with your pet while understanding and prioritizing all of your concerns.< /Review>

<Resp>None< /Resp><rating>3</rating>< text>
It was just okay.  I honestly expected more from Thai Americans in SD.

There were a number of exotic dishes that I have not tried in NYC or in LA. So I ordered an exotic curry dish with two traditional ones, tom yum soup and basil egg plant with chicken. All of them had slightly subpar taste. The soup was too sour; the basil chicken had two imperfections: the meat tasted old and the sauce lacked flavor. The exotic dish was okay but not very impressive.

I would not recommend this restaurant to my foodie friends in NYC or in LA.</text>

< Name>
Leo O</Name>
< Time>
1563939628281< /Time>
<Rate>3<//Rate>< review>
Came here with a group of 2. Was easily seated. No wait time.

For appetizers, tried the fried dumplings and Shrimp Thai wrap. The fried dumplings were pretty good. Nice balance between the flour/dough and the amount of meat you get. The Shrimp Thai wrap was underwhelming. They needed to either put in more shrimp or use a bigger size shrimp. The dish was not balanced at all and all you really eat are the vegetables. The cucumber slices were too thick. If they want to use the same amount, cut it into 2 or 3 slices.

I got the minced pork with basil with brown rice. I really wanted to like this dish but it was overly salty. The plating of this dish was excellent.

I was also able to try the Crying Tiger dish. The angus steak was incredibly dry and tough. I wouldn't recommend this dish. The plating of the food was also excellent and beautiful though.

For dessert, had the FBI. This was amazing. A great balance between ice cream and fried bananas. The honey worked well, it wasn't overly sweet. The peanuts added crunch/texture to the dish which was needed and I think they made something in the dish mildly spicy which was awesome. This was a very complete dish.  If all I had was this dish, the place would have gotten 4 stars.

The restaurant definitely has potential to put out great stuff. Perhaps I was unlucky on 4 randomly selected dishes but I may come back next time to try the curry which I've heard great things about.

Service was excellent and staff was friendly.  One thing to note is that the staff sometimes have "blinders" on. They focus on one request at a time and sometimes don't multi-task well.<//review>

<Resp>None</Resp>< text>
I really really wanted to like this restaurant so much after seeing the reviews and today being New Year's Eve.

Food - Below average . I would give no more than 2.5 stars and that's a stretch.
Service - I would give it a 0 if I could.
Ambience - Was very good. I would give it a 4-5 stars.

Again, going by the reviews, and seeing the live wait times between 15-30 mins, we decided to join the waitlist through Yelp, so we could save time.
We reached the restaurant exactly 30 mins later and mentioned that we checked in online.
The host made a face and walked away saying he'll come back. We could guess from his expression that their system was probably down and so it was obvious he wouldn't be able to find us on the wait list. Although the good thing is, he came back almost immediately and seated us. But instead of leaving us be to settle down, he lectured me about calling next time even if I used an online checkin. First of all, I have never ever called any restaurant after checkin online and have never had issues. Second of all, the tone of the host was so condescending that I was shocked. He went so far as to tell us that just because we were lucky we got a table.

We placed our drinks and main course orders together. I had  a question, to which I received a very rude answer. By this point, he had already ruined my mood.

Food arrived. Wine was pretty good. Drunken noodles were very spicy. This coming from an Indian! Red curry was underwhelming to say the least. Not much flavor at all. I have definitely had better.

Throughout the meal, no one came by to check for drink refills, neither did anyone check to see if everything was okay with our food. All the while I saw this being done at other tables around me.
I was just waiting to get out of there.
Although we wanted to eat desserts, we decided not to stay there for any more time than necessary and got the hell out.

Very very disappointed and needless to say, will never go back.<//text>

<Date>1550852504532</Date><user_id>101333935937760789718< /user_id><gmap_id>0x80d954c2b14ad255:0xa331764b2cfcda0f< /gmap_id><Review>Great place to eat, food is delicious and great ambiance</Review></record></dataset><record>
< review>
Best late night Thai in the area- open until 2am on the weekends, you really can't beat that. Parking is a pain though, best of luck on finding one.

Their top dishes are the Pad Thai, Tom Yum soup, and Massaman beef curry. Be very very careful on the spice levels, they really overdo it. Prices are pretty standard in this location- personally I think it's pricey.

They have amazing lunch specials- I'd recommend giving them a try during then.< /review>
